It is validated by the `.github/workflows/codeowners-validator.yml` CI workflow, which runs the mszostok/codeowners-validator action to check for syntax errors, duplicate patterns, and unowned files.\\n\\nGrafana integrates codeowners into its feature management system through the `codeowner` type defined in `pkg/services/featuremgmt/codeowners.go`. This type represents GitHub team or user references that match the CODEOWNERS file format. The type is used throughout the feature toggle infrastructure to track team ownership of feature flags.\\n\\nFeature toggles are defined in `pkg/services/featuremgmt/registry.go`, where each feature flag has an `Owner` field containing a codeowner constant (e.g., `@grafana/grafana-backend-group`). The `toggles_gen_test.go` test file orchestrates the generation of manifest files by running Go tests twice—the first run generates the files, the second validates them.\\n\\nThe generated manifest files include:\\n- `toggles_gen.go`: Auto-generated constants for feature flags\\n- `toggles_gen.json`: Kubernetes-style Feature resource list with codeowner information\\n- `toggles_gen.csv`: CSV export of feature toggles\\n\\nThe Kubernetes API definitions in `pkg/apis/featuretoggle/v0alpha1/types.go` include the `codeowner` field in the `FeatureSpec` struct. The `zz_generated.openapi.go` file provides OpenAPI schema definitions that reference this field.\\n\\nOn the JavaScript side, `scripts/cli/generateBettererIssues.ts` uses the `codeowners` npm package to parse the CODEOWNERS file and assign code quality issues to team owners. The `package.json` declares the `codeowners` npm dependency and the `Makefile` provides the `gen-feature-toggles` target that runs the Go tests to regenerate all manifest files when registry.go is updated.\\n\\nThe `docs/sources/setup-grafana/configure-grafana/feature-toggles/index.md` is machine-generated from the toggles_gen_test.go test and lists all available feature toggles with their codeowner information. The `contribute/feature-toggles.md` documentation guide instructs developers to define feature toggles in registry.go and run the generation tests.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1982,"cache_read_input_tokens":75941,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1982},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"772b6fe2-2b08-4077-8c93-9a0567e0b2a6","uuid":"0cf90d8a-06ec-4330-a286-fa70cfb37294"}
